// ============non-terminal types=============
//  # => Integer
//  <assign> => Statement
//  <cast exp> => Exp
//  <class decl> => ClassDecl
//  <class decl>+ => List<ClassDecl>
//  <decl in class> => Decl
//  <decl in class>* => List<Decl>
//  <empty bracket pair> => Object
//  <exp1> => Exp
//  <exp2> => Exp
//  <exp3> => Exp
//  <exp4> => Exp
//  <exp> => Exp
//  <local var decl> => Statement
//  <method decl> => Decl
//  <program> => Program
//  <start> => void
//  <stmt> => Statement
//  <stmt>* => List<Statement>
//  <super> => void
//  <type> => Type
//  <unary exp> => Exp
//  CHARLIT => Integer
//  ID => String
//  INTLIT => Integer
//  STRINGLIT => String
//  `! => void
//  `!= => void
//  `% => void
//  `&& => void
//  `( => void
//  `) => void

//  `+ => void
//  `++ => void
//  `, => void
//  `- => void

//  `. => void
//  `/ => void
//  `: => void
//  `; => void

//  `<= => void
//  `= => void
//  `== => void

//  `>= => void

// ============productions (after empty-removal)=============
// 0: $$start ::= <start>
// 1: <start> ::= ws* <program>
// 2: <start> ::= <program>
// 3: <program> ::= <class decl>+
// 4: <class decl> ::= `class ID `{ <decl in class>* `}
// 5: <class decl> ::= `class ID `{ `}
// 6: <decl in class> ::= <method decl>
// 7: <method decl> ::= `public `void ID `( `) `{ <stmt>* `}
// 8: <method decl> ::= `public `void ID `( `) `{ `}
// 9: <type> ::= `int
// 10: <type> ::= `null
// 11: <type> ::= `void
// 12: <type> ::= `boolean
// 13: <type> ::= ID
// 14: <type> ::= <type> <empty bracket pair>
// 15: <empty bracket pair> ::= `[ `]
// 16: <stmt> ::= <assign> `;
// 17: <stmt> ::= `{ <stmt>* `}
// 18: <stmt> ::= `{ `}
// 19: <stmt> ::= <local var decl> `;
// 20: <stmt> ::= `break `;
// 21: <assign> ::= <exp> `= <exp>
// 22: <local var decl> ::= <type> ID `= <exp>
// 23: <exp> ::= <exp4>
// 24: <exp4> ::= `true
// 25: <exp4> ::= `false
// 26: <exp4> ::= <exp4> `+ <exp3>
// 27: <exp3> ::= <exp3> `- <exp2>
// 28: <exp4> ::= <exp3>
// 29: <exp3> ::= <exp3> `* <exp2>
// 30: <exp3> ::= <exp3> `/ <exp2>
// 31: <exp3> ::= <exp3> `% <exp2>
// 32: <exp3> ::= <exp3> `&& <exp2>
// 33: <exp3> ::= <exp2>
// 34: <exp2> ::= <cast exp>
// 35: <exp2> ::= <unary exp>
// 36: <cast exp> ::= `( <type> `) <cast exp>
// 37: <cast exp> ::= `( <type> `) <exp1>
// 38: <exp3> ::= <exp3> `instanceof <type>
// 39: <unary exp> ::= `- <unary exp>
// 40: <unary exp> ::= <exp1>
// 41: <exp1> ::= ID
// 42: <exp1> ::= <exp1> !<empty bracket pair> `[ <exp> `]
// 43: <exp1> ::= INTLIT
// 44: <exp1> ::= STRINGLIT
// 45: letter ::= {"A".."Z" "a".."z"}
// 46: letter128 ::= {193..218 225..250}
// 47: digit ::= {"0".."9"}
// 48: digit128 ::= {176..185}
// 49: any ::= {0..127}
// 50: any128 ::= {128..255}
// 51: ws ::= " "
// 52: ws ::= {10}
// 53: `boolean ::= "#" "b" "o" ws*
// 54: `boolean ::= "#" "b" "o"
// 55: `class ::= "#" "c" "l" ws*
// 56: `class ::= "#" "c" "l"
// 57: `void ::= "#" "v" "o" ws*
// 58: `void ::= "#" "v" "o"
// 59: `int ::= "#" "i" "t" ws*
// 60: `int ::= "#" "i" "t"
// 61: `break ::= "#" "b" "r" ws*
// 62: `break ::= "#" "b" "r"
// 63: `false ::= "#" "f" "a" ws*
// 64: `false ::= "#" "f" "a"
// 65: `true ::= "#" "t" "r" ws*
// 66: `true ::= "#" "t" "r"
// 67: `null ::= "#" "n" "u" ws*
// 68: `null ::= "#" "n" "u"
// 69: `instanceof ::= "#" "i" "n" ws*
// 70: `instanceof ::= "#" "i" "n"
// 71: `public ::= "#" "p" "u" ws*
// 72: `public ::= "#" "p" "u"
// 73: `% ::= "%" ws*
// 74: `% ::= "%"
// 75: `&& ::= "@" "&" ws*
// 76: `&& ::= "@" "&"
// 77: `* ::= "*" ws*
// 78: `* ::= "*"
// 79: `( ::= "(" ws*
// 80: `( ::= "("
// 81: `) ::= ")" ws*
// 82: `) ::= ")"
// 83: `{ ::= "{" ws*
// 84: `{ ::= "{"
// 85: `} ::= "}" ws*
// 86: `} ::= "}"
// 87: `- ::= "-" ws*
// 88: `- ::= "-"
// 89: `+ ::= "+" ws*
// 90: `+ ::= "+"
// 91: `= ::= "=" ws*
// 92: `= ::= "="
// 93: `[ ::= "[" ws*
// 94: `[ ::= "["
// 95: `] ::= "]" ws*
// 96: `] ::= "]"
// 97: `; ::= ";" ws*
// 98: `; ::= ";"
// 99: `/ ::= "/" ws*
// 100: `/ ::= "/"
// 101: ID ::= letter128 ws*
// 102: ID ::= letter128
// 103: ID ::= letter idChar* $$0
// 104: ID ::= letter $$0
// 105: INTLIT ::= {"1".."9"} digit* $$1
// 106: INTLIT ::= {"1".."9"} $$1
// 107: INTLIT ::= digit128 ws*
// 108: INTLIT ::= digit128
// 109: INTLIT ::= "0" hexDigit* $$2
// 110: INTLIT ::= "0" $$2
// 111: STRINGLIT ::= "@" '"' ws*
// 112: STRINGLIT ::= "@" '"'
// 113: STRINGLIT ::= '"' any* $$3
// 114: STRINGLIT ::= '"' $$3
// 115: idChar ::= letter
// 116: idChar ::= digit
// 117: idChar ::= "_"
// 118: idChar128 ::= letter128
// 119: idChar128 ::= digit128
// 120: idChar128 ::= {223}
// 121: hexDigit ::= {"0".."9" "A".."Z" "a".."z"}
// 122: hexDigit128 ::= {176..185 193..198 225..230}
// 123: digit* ::= digit* digit
// 124: digit* ::= digit
// 125: any* ::= any* any
// 126: any* ::= any
// 127: <decl in class>* ::= <decl in class>* <decl in class>
// 128: <decl in class>* ::= <decl in class>
// 129: hexDigit* ::= hexDigit* hexDigit
// 130: hexDigit* ::= hexDigit
// 131: <stmt>* ::= <stmt>* <stmt>
// 132: <stmt>* ::= <stmt>
// 133: idChar* ::= idChar* idChar
// 134: idChar* ::= idChar
// 135: <class decl>+ ::= <class decl>
// 136: <class decl>+ ::= <class decl>+ <class decl>
// 137: ws* ::= ws* ws
// 138: ws* ::= ws
// 139: $$0 ::= idChar128 ws*
// 140: $$0 ::= idChar128
// 141: $$1 ::= digit128 ws*
// 142: $$1 ::= digit128
// 143: $$2 ::= hexDigit128 ws*
// 144: $$2 ::= hexDigit128
// 145: $$3 ::= any128 ws*
// 146: $$3 ::= any128

**** STATE 0 ****
    $$start ::= <%> <start> // $
    -----------------------
    <class decl> ::= <%> `class [#] ID `{ <decl in class>* `} // $
    <class decl> ::= <%> `class [#] ID `{ <decl in class>* `} // <class decl>
    <class decl> ::= <%> `class [#] ID `{ [<decl in class>*] `} // $
    <class decl> ::= <%> `class [#] ID `{ [<decl in class>*] `} // <class decl>
    <class decl>+ ::= <%> <class decl> // $
    <class decl>+ ::= <%> <class decl> // <class decl>
    <class decl>+ ::= <%> <class decl>+ <class decl> // $
    <class decl>+ ::= <%> <class decl>+ <class decl> // <class decl>
    <program> ::= [#] <%> <class decl>+ // $
    <start> ::= <%> ws* <program> // $
    <start> ::= [ws*] <%> <program> // $
    `class ::= <%> "#" "c" "l" [ws*] // ID
    `class ::= <%> "#" "c" "l" ws* // ID
    ws ::= <%> " " // <program>
    ws ::= <%> " " // ws
    ws ::= <%> {10} [registerNewline] // <program>
    ws ::= <%> {10} [registerNewline] // ws
    ws* ::= <%> ws* ws // <program>
    ws* ::= <%> ws* ws // ws
    ws* ::= [ws*] <%> ws // <program>
    ws* ::= [ws*] <%> ws // ws
        <class decl>+ => shift: 56
        "#" => shift: 180
        ws => shift: 260
        <program> => shift: 138
        `class => shift: 83
        <start> => shift: 223
        ws* => shift: 291
        {10} => shift: 24
        " " => shift: 78
        <class decl> => shift: 208

**** STATE 6 ****
    <local var decl> ::= <type> [#] ID `= <%> <exp> // `;
    -----------------------
    <cast exp> ::= [#] <%> `( <type> `) <cast exp> // `%
    <cast exp> ::= [#] <%> `( <type> `) <cast exp> // `&&
    <cast exp> ::= [#] <%> `( <type> `) <cast exp> // `*

    <cast exp> ::= [#] <%> `( <type> `) <exp1> // `%
